 Launching from the Satish Dhawan Space Center, the Indian Space Research Organization (ISRO) said that the 'IRNSS-1E' would be launched from the second launch pad of Satish Dhawan inter-station of Sriharikota, about 100 km from Chennai at 9:31 am
 do tarah ke pelod le jayegiserone bataaya ki ‘IRNSS-1E’ apane saath do tarah ke pelod (antariksh upkaran) lekar jayega, jisamen ek nevigation, jabaki doosraa reging pelod hoga
 The navigation payload will send the signals connected to the navigation service to the users and it will work in 'L-5' and 'S' bands
 lager ke jariye range kaa pataa chalegaraging pelod main ‘si’ band kaa ek transponder laga hoga, jisase upgrah kii range ke bare main sateek jaankaree mil sakegi
 The IRNSS-1E will also carry a corner cube retro reflectors to explore the range through a laser
 atyant sateek ‘rubidium parmaanu ghadi’ upgrah ke nevigation pelod kaa hissaa he

 udaan kii shuruyaat ke vakt ‘iareneses-1i’ kaa dravyaman 1425 kilogram he

 Dr

 sarkaar kii ye yojana neem hakim ko vaid karne kii sajeesh he

 isse jhola chhap doctor bhi vaid ho jaaenge

 GD Agarwal has made his life home
 isi kadi main haryana ke ek sadhu sant gopaldaas ne rishikesh main triveni ghat main buudhvaar se ann jal tyaag diya he
 He started a fast in Badrinath from 24 June
 prashasan unhen jabaran ames rishikesh le aayaa or tab se wo rishikesh main anshan par hai or ab unhone jal bhi tyaag diya he
 The question is whether Ganga will survive or will one more know
 ab ganga kii baat kyon nahin ho rahi he, us par vigyaapan kyon nahin aa rahe hai, mantriyon ke twit kyon nahin aa rahe hai

 ganga ke liye koi naaraa laga de, khabar ban jaaegi, koi jaan de de, khabar gaayab ho jaaegi
 Although the people of Matrasadan and Prof
 jidi agarwal ke jaanane waalon ko lagata he ki unki mrityu ke kaarnon kii jaanch honi chahie
 Pro
 jidi agarwal kaa nidhan ek vyakti kaa nidhan nahin he
 This is the demise of an institution, Prof
 agarwal ne pradhanmantri ko kai baar patr likhaa
 They wanted to see something solid
 ji di agarwal ganga ko lekar sarkaar ko uske vaade kii lagaataar yaad dilaate rahe
 Keep saying that the river Ganga should be made continuous, the dam should be stopped in its path, illegal mining should be stopped on the banks of the Ganga, the dirt falling in the Ganga should be stopped
 iske liye ganga ko lekar ek kaanoon banaaya jaae jiskaa ek draft unhone centre sarkaar ko bheja bhi tha
 But on Tuesday, there was no concrete assurance that the Uttarakhand Chief Minister Ramesh Pokhriyal Nishank brought with him Ganga and Water Resources Minister Nitin Gadkari to break his fast on Tuesday
 unhone jal tyaag kar diya
 More than 5000 people died in the terrible disaster of 2013, followed by several scientific reports that said that many concrete decisions would have to be taken to save the Ganges but none were implemented
 2014 main van or paryaavaran mantralay kii report supreme court main daakhil kii gai jisamen kaha gaya tha ki hydro power projects ne 2013 kii aapadaa ko badhaane main aag main ghi kaa kaam kiya he
 The report recommended a ban on dams being built in the Ganges basin
 2016 main khud ganga mantralay ne supreme court main daakhil halafanaame main kaha ki baandhon se ganga ko jo nuksaan hua he uski bharpai nahin kii ja sakati
 Therefore, it is necessary to stop the dams
 lekin sarkaar ne inhen gambhirtha se nahin liya
 The situation today is that there are seventy dam projects in the basins of Alakanda, Mandakini and Bhagirathi
 inamen se 19 to puri ho chuki hai
 The loss of not enough flow from these dams is clearly visible
 iske alaava 17 chote-bade baandhon ko banane kaa kaam chal rahaa he, inamen chaar bade baandh bhi hai
 24 dams are proposed on the Ganges, which is currently under a Supreme Court stay
 ye banpar tu banpar baandh ganga kaa galaa ghontne ko aatur hai
 There are many more reports that warn against the delicate ecology of the Ganges and the Himalayas, and are refusing to play with the Ganges
 2010 main tab ke yojana ayog ne himalayan rajyon ke liye jibi mukherjee task force cameti banaai thi
 This committee had said that there should be no tampering around water sources in Himalayan areas
 himalay ko rajasav ugaahne kaa zariyaa nahin banaaya janaa chahie
 In 2012, WII stated that hydropower projects would prove to be very bad for wild life
 2013 main centre sarkaar ke kai mantralayon se judi chaturvedi cameti kii report ne kaha tha ki ganga kii kuch sahaayak nadiyon ko pristine form main chhod dena chahie yani jaisi wo hameshaa se bahati rahi hai waisi
 They should not be tampered with at all
 neshnal institute of dizaster management kii ek report main kaha gaya tha ki uttarakhand kii vikaas nitiyon ne dizaster ke liye ek parfect racipe taiyaar kii he
 The construction of roads, construction of dams, indiscriminate tourism in the state were blamed for the disaster
 2014 main ravi chopra cameti ne saafe kaha tha ki ganga par bane sabhi baandhon ne apurnty kshati pahunchaai he
 Many well-known scientists and experts were included in this committee, but the government also put it on the back burner
 isi saal kii shuruyaat main niti ayog ne kaha ki himalay main pani ke 60% strot sookhne kii kagaar par pahunch gaye hai
 This year's Forest Survey of India report says that the forest area is decreasing above one thousand meters
 july 2018 neshnal beuro of soyal survey and land yuz planning, nagpur kii report ai he jisamen kaha gaya he ki qareeb aadha uttarakhand ati gambhir bhu kataav kii jad main he or mitti kaa ye kataav tolerance limit se upar he
 The worst situation is in the catchment area of the Ganges
 yahaan 40 se 80 ton prati hectare prati varsh kii dar se bhu kataav ho rahaa he jo gambhir shrenee main he
 The comments sabko sab dikh rahaa he magar udyogpatiyon, thekedaaron or netaaon ke nexs ke bich vikaas naam kii chandani main ganga kisi ko nahin dikhti he
 Due to this nexus, the government and governments have not been able to get the Kumbh area in Haridwar to be mined free while the Central Pollution Control Board has imposed a ban on mining here by imposing section five
 baandhon ke alaava chaar dham pariyojna ke naam par sadak ke chaudeekaran kaa project ganga ko barbaad kar rahaa he
 Where debris is being dumped in the Ganges

 is report main ganga nadi ke basin main ban rahe baandhon par roak lagane kii sifaarish kii gai
 In 2016, the Ganga Ministry itself in an affidavit filed in the Supreme Court said that the damage done to the Ganges by the dams cannot be compensated
 isliye baandhon par roak lagani zaruri he

 har din ho rahi khoj maut ko pachhad rahi he

 rassakashi darasal allopathic ke puraane pairokaron or vividh prakaar ke prakritik ilaaj kii ore rukh kar rahe nae rujhaan ke bich chal rahi he, jinhen mote taur par poorak or vaikalpik chikitsa (cam) kaha jaataa he yaa zyada nae rup main ise integrated medicine yaa samanvayakaari chikitsa kehete hai

 'machhliyon ke marane ke peeche pani main oxigen kii kami kii ashanka jataai ja rahi he

 vaise samay-samay par gomti ke pani main oxigen kii maatra kii jaanch karai jaati he
